Ticket: PFT-2933
Issue id: 180831
Module: Data & Reporting
Summary: Exporting Behaviour logs and SEN Notes
Role: Trust IT Manager
Source: Sheet1 - Row 23
Comment: I'm writing to request consideration for a new feature or product that would significantly improve our ability to manage student behaviour data within the trust.

 Currently, when we move a student to a different school within our trust due to behaviour issues, we face a major challenge. The Common Transfer File (CTF), as defined by the DfE, doesn't include Special Educational Needs (SEN) notes or detailed behaviour incident data. This means that when a student transfers, the receiving school has no way to access their historical behaviour patterns or SEN information directly.

 Our only workaround is for staff at the new school to manually re-enter every single behaviour incident and SEN note into their Arbor system. This is an incredibly time-consuming process and creates a significant administrative burden. More importantly, it delays the new school's ability to understand the student's existing needs and behaviour triggers, which is crucial for providing effective support and intervention from day one.

 Implementing a solution that allows for the secure and efficient transfer of this vital behaviour and SEN data between Arbor instances within our trust would be a game-changer. It would not only save countless staff hours but, more importantly, empower our schools to more quickly identify and address a student's behaviour trigger points, leading to better outcomes for our pupils.

 Could you please investigate potential solutions for this data transfer challenge? I believe this would be a high-impact development for our trust.

 Thanks,

Ticket: PFT-2888
Issue id: 180607
Module: Payments
Summary: Allow trips to carry over to the next academic year/remove minimum instalment amount
Role: PA to the Headteacher
Source: Sheet1 - Row 68
Comment: As most secondary schools do, we often create trips for the next academic year to allow parents to pay the cost of the trip however Arbor does not allow us to set a trip date outside of the current year. The current set up is also messy for audit purposes as it looks as though the same trip has occurred multiple times and makes it difficult to track payments.

 The minimum instalment amount should also be removed as we should be able to simply tick that instalments are allowed - parents can decide the minimum they want to pay per instalment.

 https://support.arbor-education.com/hc/en-us/articles/9710262266397-Create-and-send-out-Custom-Report-Cards#h_01H95EGQ5JJZXGB996B28XWR52

 FAQs

 Can we do conditional formatting or colour-coding?

 You can apply conditional formatting to a report in the Custom Report Writer to colour code fields in the report.

 This conditional formatting will not be pulled through to the merge fields used in your Custom Report Card. As such, you cannot colour-code fields in the Custom Report card based on data.

This added layer of awareness could be particularly vital in preventing missed doses and ensuring the consistent care of students on short-term medication.

Ticket: PFT-2412
Issue id: 179062
Module: Report Cards
Summary: Report card to include student information and subject information for leavers YR13
Role: Data Administrator
Source: Sheet1 - Row 544
Comment: We either need through Report card or through Custom report Writer a college leaver's form

 Firstly each form need headings of name of student, DOB, TG(form group)

 then Subjects (normally x3), subject teachers in a table.to allow subject teachers signatures next to each subject taken.

 below is the feedback from my request, which I believe does tell you everything we need.

 "I'm just getting back to you around your college leavers form.

 To recall, you were using a custom report card in Arbor to create a college leavers form - essentially a checklist for students to confirm that they'd handed in keys and got signatures from their subject teachers

 As we covered in the call, a custom report is created with a focus. This dictates what fields are available in the custom report, but also what those fields are in relation to - if you create a report about students then all the information will be in relation to the students, but if you create a custom report about courses then the report will be in relation to the courses. This was why your custom report has the student names in multiple times, as report is looking at the courses you entered and which students are in them - as each student is in multiple courses they'l show up alongside each course in the report.

 Because the report you created is about course enrolments it won't pull across the information in the format that is needed for it to pulled into a custom report card.

 Because you're using the custom report card in a slightly unusual way (as in, this isn't what they're intended for, but I recognise that they're similar) I don't think it's possible to get all the information you need in the leavers form in by using the custom report cards.

 Unfortunately, I think that it's likely going to be primarily out-of-Arbor work to get this done in the way you're looking for. While you can make the template in Arbor - something you've already done - Arbor won't be able to pull across the specific subject teacher, just the academic lead for the topic.

 In this instance I would advise creating the report out of Arbor, or printing the template that you've created in Arbor and filling in the relevant section outside of Arbor. I would also recommend leaving product feedback, as I would expect that a leaver checklist/form would be doable in Arbor; I'll put details of product feedback below":

Ticket: PFT-2250
Issue id: 178427
Module: Attendance
Summary: Bradford Factor Calculation
Role: Data Manager
Source: Sheet1 - Row 706
Comment: Hi

 Your Bradford Factor calculation needs to be changed.

 Currently your Calculation:

 The score is calculated using the formula: Bradford Factor = (Number of Absences)¬≤ x Total Days Absent.

 It would be more useful:-

 the number of absence days squared multiplied by the number of incidences of absence.

 Named after Bradford University where it originated in the 1980s, the Bradford Factor is based on the theory that shorter, more frequent absences are more detrimental to an organization than longer, less frequent ones.

 This is also true in schools, frequent five odd days off are more detrimental than one week period of absence.

 Identifying the odd days off is the purpose of the Bradford factor so the underlying causes can be addressed.

 Please can you change your calculation.

Ticket: PFT-2206
Issue id: 178194
Module: Data & Reporting
Summary: Reference Numbers & Bulk Search
Role: System Development Lead, HISP Multi Academy Trust
Source: Sheet1 - Row 750
Comment: As long-time users of Integris (now owned by Arbor), our staff have grown accustomed to and reliant on having admin, reference, and student ID numbers displayed alongside student names. This feature not only helps distinguish between students with the same name but also proves invaluable for data analysis. While we appreciate that Arbor allows searching by student ID, it only supports individual searches and bulk searching is not currently possible. Additionally, these ID numbers are still not displayed in search results or clearly alongside student names in profiles or reports. Losing this functionality would represent a significant setback for both our administrative and teaching staff, substantially increasing their workload.

 We would also benefit greatly from a way to rapidly select multiple students from lists provided externally or of a completely ad-hoc nature. For example, we are often given lists of, say, 86 students across multiple year groups for University Experience Days. In such cases, we do not want to manually search for each student by name or select them from a full list of students across the school or year group. A fast, efficient method for selecting students from external lists (preferably by bulk searching reference numbers, as was possible in Integris) would significantly enhance our ability to manage events, create custom groups for communication, and reduce the administrative burden that would otherwise increase if we were to transition fully to Arbor in its current form.

 A video clip demonstrating this functionality in Integris can be provided on request.

Additionally, these ID numbers are still not displayed in search results or clearly alongside student names in profiles or reports. Losing this functionality would represent a significant setback for both our administrative and teaching staff, substantially increasing their workload.

 We would also benefit greatly from a way to rapidly select multiple students from lists provided externally or of a completely ad-hoc nature. For example, we are often given lists of, say, 86 students across multiple year groups for University Experience Days. In such cases, we do not want to manually search for each student by name or select them from a full list of students across the school or year group. A fast, efficient method for selecting students from external lists (preferably by bulk searching reference numbers, as was possible in Integris) would significantly enhance our ability to manage events, create custom groups for communication, and reduce the administrative burden that would otherwise increase if we were to transition fully to Arbor in its current form.

 A video clip demonstrating this functionality in Integris can be provided on request.

Summary: Attendance fines

Additionally, the fact that the options are only 'issued' or 'waived' is not ideal. 'Other' would be very helpful, for example, if the case were complex and a Legal Intervention Team referral was the course of action required.

Issue id: 177929
Module: Attendance
Summary: Manually Update Roll Call Marks
Role: Unknown
Source: Sheet1 - Row 812
Comment: Please can you help to make this change (urgently if possible).

 (This doesn't apply to KS3/4)

 Our parameters for picking up roll call marks are lessons one and five and we will not be changing these.

 Some of our Sixth Form students do not have a lesson until after lesson one, therefore, their roll call mark will remain blank.

 In our previous system we were able to manually update students' roll call marks retrospectively. If we are unable to complete the roll call marks the system will read these missing marks as the student being absent thus drastically reducing students' overall percentage attendance, affecting our returns to the LEA.

 I hope you understand, and I look forward to hearing from you.

 Thank you very much for considering this change.

 Kind regards

 Susan Adams

 Sixth Form Coordinator

 Stanwell School

 Tel: 029 2070 7633

Role: Director of Operations
Source: Sheet1 - Row 826
Comment: Top Line - please had a default option in custom report writer to pull data for "two weeks prior", in addition to the options for "current week" and "last week". This would be awesome, thank you!

 Hi,

 I have just been on chat with one of your team and we realised that I want is not currently possible so it was recommend i feed back here.

 On a Monday morning we review summary performance data across the Trust. Attendance is a strategic priority as it will be for all Trusts.

 We want to focus on incremental / marginal improvements, and therefore our data set looks at marginal gains week on week.

 In the custom report I have built, the parameters are for "current week attendance" and "last week attendance".

 However, as we are looking at this on a Monday morning, the data in "current week attendance" is showing registrations for Monday AM only, therefore not giving us a meaningful view.

 Whilst I could set a custom date range, showing "last week" and "two weeks ago", this would need to be updated manually for every school every week which is not ideal.

 So, what I think would be brilliant is if you can add an extra pre-set option, like "current week" and "las week" that is "2 weeks prior".

 Hope that makes sense, and hope you can roll this out as soon as possible.... next week?!?!

 Regards,

 Jon.
